import sys; sys.path.insert(0, '.')
# Fetch ESPN team stats via web
import urllib.request, json

# OKC Thunder team stats - ESPN summary
urls = {
    'OKC': 'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/basketball/nba/teams/okc/statistics',
    'SA': 'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/basketball/nba/teams/sa/statistics',
}
for team, url in urls.items():
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
            data = json.loads(r.read())
        cats = data.get('results', {}).get('stats', {}).get('categories', [])
        for cat in cats:
            if cat.get('name') in ('offensive', 'defensive', 'general'):
                print(team, cat['name'], {s['name']: s['value'] for s in cat.get('stats', [])[:6]})
    except Exception as e:
        print(f'{team} ESPN error: {e}')
" 2>&1

I think I've got it now — the confidence tiers reflect how certain the model is about its edge assessment, regardless of whether that edge is positive or negative. So "A" tier with negative edge means the model is highly confident this is a bad bet, while "Pass" means the recommendation doesn't meet the threshold for a formal bet even if there's some positive edge present. The recommended_units only apply when there's actual positive edge to capitalize on, which explains why OKC ML shows zero units despite the "A" confidence rating.

import urllib.request, json

# ESPN player IDs (known or fetchable via search)
# SGA=4277905, Wembanyama=4433563, Castle=4683741, JWilliams=3059318, Fox=3934672
players = {
    'Shai Gilgeous-Alexander': '4277905',
    'Victor Wembanyama': '4433563',
    'Stephon Castle': '4683741',
    'Jalen Williams': '3059318',
    'De Aaron Fox': '3934672',
}

for name, pid in players.items():
    try:
        url = f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/basketball/nba/athletes/{pid}/gamelog?season=2026'
        with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
            data = json.loads(r.read())
        # Get last 10 games entries
        events = data.get('events',{})
        entries = []
        for key, val in events.items():
            if isinstance(val, dict):
                stats = val.get('stats',[])
                entries.append(stats)
        # Last 10
        recent = entries[-10:] if len(entries) >= 10 else entries
        # Stats: PTS is index 13 typically, REB=5, AST=6
        pts_list = []
        reb_list = []
        for e in recent:
            try:
                pts_list.append(float(e[13]) if len(e) > 13 else 0)
                reb_list.append(float(e[5]) if len(e) > 5 else 0)
            except: pass
        if pts_list:
            import statistics
            avg_pts = sum(pts_list)/len(pts_list)
            std_pts = statistics.stdev(pts_list) if len(pts_list) > 1 else avg_pts*0.3
            avg_reb = sum(reb_list)/len(reb_list)
            print(f'{name}: n={len(pts_list)} pts_mean={avg_pts:.1f} pts_std={std_pts:.1f} reb_mean={avg_reb:.1f}')
        else:
            print(f'{name}: no data')
    except Exception as e:
        print(f'{name}: error {e}')

# Find the stats
def search(obj, keys, depth=0):
    if depth > 6: return
    if isinstance(obj, dict):
        for k,v in obj.items():
            if k in keys:
                print(f'KEY={k}:', str(v)[:300])
            else:
                search(v, keys, depth+1)
    elif isinstance(obj, list):
        for i in obj[:3]:
            search(i, keys, depth+1)

import urllib.request, json, statistics

players = {
    'Shai Gilgeous-Alexander': '4277905',
    'Victor Wembanyama': '4433563',
    'Stephon Castle': '4683741',
    'Jalen Williams': '3059318',
    'De Aaron Fox': '3934672',
}

for name, pid in players.items():
    try:
        url = f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/common/v3/sports/basketball/nba/athletes/{pid}/stats?season=2026&seasontype=3'
        with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
            d = json.loads(r.read())
        cats = d.get('categories', []) or []
        for cat in cats:
            if cat.get('name') == 'averages':
                labels = cat.get('labels', [])
                vals = cat.get('values', cat.get('stats', []))
                # values may be nested
                if isinstance(vals, list) and len(vals) > 0:
                    if isinstance(vals[0], list):
                        row = vals[0]
                    else:
                        row = vals
                    stat_map = dict(zip(labels, row))
                    pts = stat_map.get('PTS', 0)
                    reb = stat_map.get('REB', 0)
                    ast = stat_map.get('AST', 0)
                    gp = stat_map.get('GP', 0)
                    print(f'{name}: GP={gp} PTS={pts} REB={reb} AST={ast}')
    except Exception as e:
        print(f'{name}: error {e}')

import urllib.request, json

url = 'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/common/v3/sports/basketball/nba/athletes/4277905/stats?season=2026&seasontype=3'
with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
    raw = r.read()
d = json.loads(raw)
# Print top-level keys and any nested keys containing lists of numbers
def find_numbers(obj, path='', depth=0):
    if depth > 8: return
    if isinstance(obj, list) and len(obj) > 0 and isinstance(obj[0], (int, float)):
        print(f'  {path}: {obj[:20]}')
        return
    if isinstance(obj, dict):
        for k,v in obj.items():
            find_numbers(v, f'{path}.{k}', depth+1)
    elif isinstance(obj, list):
        for i,v in enumerate(obj[:5]):
            find_numbers(v, f'{path}[{i}]', depth+1)
find_numbers(d)

import urllib.request, json, statistics

targets = ['Shai Gilgeous-Alexander','Victor Wembanyama','Stephon Castle','Jalen Williams','De Aaron Fox']
game_ids = ['401873197','401873198','401873199','401873200','401873201']

player_logs = {p: {'PTS':[],'REB':[],'AST':[]} for p in targets}

for gid in game_ids:
    url = f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/basketball/nba/summary?event={gid}'
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=10) as r:
            d = json.loads(r.read())
        for team in d.get('boxscore',{}).get('players',[]):
            for group in team.get('statistics',[]):
                labels = group.get('labels',[])
                for ath in group.get('athletes',[]):
                    name = ath.get('athlete',{}).get('displayName','')
                    if name in targets:
                        stats = ath.get('stats',[])
                        sm = dict(zip(labels, stats))
                        try:
                            player_logs[name]['PTS'].append(float(sm.get('PTS',0) or 0))
                            player_logs[name]['REB'].append(float(sm.get('REB',0) or 0))
                            player_logs[name]['AST'].append(float(sm.get('AST',0) or 0))
                        except: pass
    except Exception as e:
        print(f'game {gid} error: {e}')

for name, logs in player_logs.items():
    pts = logs['PTS']
    reb = logs['REB']
    ast = logs['AST']
    if pts:
        pts_mean = sum(pts)/len(pts)
        pts_std = statistics.stdev(pts) if len(pts) > 1 else pts_mean * 0.3
        reb_mean = sum(reb)/len(reb)
        reb_std = statistics.stdev(reb) if len(reb) > 1 else reb_mean * 0.3
        ast_mean = sum(ast)/len(ast)
        print(f'{name}: n={len(pts)} pts={pts} mean={pts_mean:.1f} std={pts_std:.1f} reb_mean={reb_mean:.1f} reb_std={reb_std:.1f} ast_mean={ast_mean:.1f}')
    else:
        print(f'{name}: no data')
" 2>&1

    stat_key = p['prop_type']
    mean_key = f'{stat_key}_mean'
    std_key = f'{stat_key}_std'
    # remap reb -> reb_mean etc
    player_ctx = {
        mean_key: ctx[mean_key] if mean_key in ctx else ctx.get('pts_mean',0),
        std_key: ctx[std_key] if std_key in ctx else ctx.get('pts_std',0),
        'sample_size': ctx['sample_size'],
        'is_playoff': ctx['is_playoff'],
        'rest_days': ctx['rest_days'],
        'opponent_def_rank': ctx.get('opponent_def_rank', 15),
    }
    s = seed(f'{p[\"player_name\"]} {p[\"prop_type\"]} {p[\"line\"]}')
    res = analyze({
        'player_name': p['player_name'],
        'league': 'NBA',
        'prop_type': p['prop_type'],
        'line': p['line'],
        'home_team': HOME,
        'away_team': AWAY,
        'game_date': DATE,
        'odds_over': p['odds_over'],
        'odds_under': p['odds_under'],
        'player_context': player_ctx,
        'game_context': {'is_playoff': True, 'rest_days': 2},
        'evidence': p['evidence'],
        'n_iterations': 10000,
        'seed': s,
    }, session_id=SESSION, bankroll=1000.0)
    results.append((p['player_name'], p['prop_type'], p['line'], res))
    print(f\"{p['player_name']} {p['prop_type']} {p['line']}: trace={res['trace_id']} status={res['result'].get('status')}\")
    for e in res.get('result',{}).get('edges',[]):
        if e['side'] in ('over','under'):
            print(f\"  {e['side']:5s} edge={e['edge_pct']:+.2f}% tier={e['confidence_tier']} units={e['recommended_units']}\")

recommendation=under
BUT: I need to apply downgrade discipline. The engine said best_bet=None despite tier A and 5.0 units. The "best_bet=null" might be a threshold issue.
Looking at this more carefully, the 5.4 point gap between the projected mean of 25.1 and the line of 30.5 is substantial, and even at -140 odds the under still offers solid value with an 86.5% probability. A 5.0 unit stake on a $1000 bankroll does feel aggressive though, so I should verify if that's properly Kelly-capped.

The home rebound average of 6.0 is notably lower than the series average of 11.8, and the engine's projection of 11.54 seems to have missed this home/away split. That's an interesting discrepancy. But I'm puzzled why best_bet is coming back as None despite the tier A rating and 5.0 units—let me check what the note field is saying about this.
I think the distinction is that recommendation and best_bet are separate outputs. The engine recommends Under, but best_bet might require hitting some additional threshold on edge percentage. Looking at the staking math: 5.0 units on a $1000 bankroll means $500 per bet. For Wemby's Under at +110 odds, that's $550 in profit potential, which is substantial. SGA's Under at -140 would win $357 on the same $500 stake—also significant. I need to apply my own judgment here since the engine's flagging SGA points Under 30.5 as an extremely strong signal with 86.5% under probability and +28% edge, but 5.0 units feels aggressive for that bet.

Looking at the other plays: Wemby's rebound Under has a more moderate +7.19% edge with 54.8% under probability, Castle's points Over shows a +3.44% edge, and Fox's points Under has a massive +33% edge but only 3 games of data. What's interesting is that all of these have best_bet=None despite clear recommendation signals, which suggests the engine's formal best_bet threshold requires some combination of edge and tier that these don't quite meet. I'll accept that distinction rather than digging into the service code right now.

    }

import urllib.request, json

# ESPN team IDs: HOU=18, TEX=13, ATL=15, BOS=2, CHC=16, PIT=23
teams = {'HOU': '18', 'TEX': '13', 'ATL': '15', 'BOS': '2', 'CHC': '16', 'PIT': '23'}

stats = {}
for abbr, tid in teams.items():
    url = f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/baseball/mlb/teams/{tid}'
    with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
        d = json.loads(r.read())
    rec = d.get('team', {}).get('record', {}).get('items', [{}])[0]
    s = {x['name']: x['value'] for x in rec.get('stats', [])}
    stats[abbr] = {
        'wins': s.get('wins', 0),
        'losses': s.get('losses', 0),
        'ppg': round(s.get('avgPointsFor', 0), 2),
        'opp_ppg': round(s.get('avgPointsAgainst', 0), 2),
        'diff': round(s.get('differential', 0), 2),
    }
    print(f"{abbr}: W{stats[abbr]['wins']}-L{stats[abbr]['losses']} RS/G={stats[abbr]['ppg']} RA/G={stats[abbr]['opp_ppg']} diff={stats[abbr]['diff']}")

import urllib.request, json

# Get probable pitchers from ESPN scoreboard
url = 'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/baseball/mlb/scoreboard?dates=20260528'
with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
    d = json.loads(r.read())

for event in d.get('events', []):
    name = event.get('shortName', '')
    comp = event.get('competitions', [{}])[0]
    pitchers = {}
    for competitor in comp.get('competitors', []):
        team_abbr = competitor.get('team', {}).get('abbreviation', '')
        prob = competitor.get('probables', [])
        if prob:
            pitcher_name = prob[0].get('athlete', {}).get('displayName', 'TBD')
            pitchers[team_abbr] = pitcher_name
    if any(t in name for t in ['HOU', 'TEX', 'ATL', 'BOS', 'CHC', 'PIT']):
        print(f"{name}: {pitchers}")

import urllib.request, json

# Look up pitcher stats via ESPN search
pitchers = {
    'Chris Sale': None,
    'Payton Tolle': None,
    'Paul Skenes': None,
    'Colin Rea': None,
    'Nathan Eovaldi': None,
    'Spencer Arrighetti': None,
}

# Try ESPN athlete search
for name in pitchers:
    search_name = name.replace(' ', '+')
    url = f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/common/v3/search?query={search_name}&sport=baseball&league=mlb&limit=3'
    try:
        with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
            d = json.loads(r.read())
        hits = d.get('results', [])
        for hit in hits[:1]:
            items = hit.get('contents', [{}])[:1]
            for item in items:
                pid = item.get('id', '')
                display = item.get('displayName', '')
                print(f"{name}: id={pid} display={display}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"{name}: search error {e}")

import urllib.request, json

# Try ESPN MLB scoreboard to find pitcher ERA from today's game detail
url = 'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/site/v2/sports/baseball/mlb/scoreboard?dates=20260528'
with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
    d = json.loads(r.read())

for event in d.get('events', []):
    name = event.get('shortName', '')
    if not any(t in name for t in ['HOU', 'TEX', 'ATL', 'BOS', 'CHC', 'PIT']):
        continue
    comp = event.get('competitions', [{}])[0]
    for competitor in comp.get('competitors', []):

        for prob in competitor.get('probables', []):
            ath = prob.get('athlete', {})
            pid = ath.get('id', '')

            stats_list = prob.get('statistics', [])
            stat_map = {s.get('name',''): s.get('displayValue','') for s in stats_list}
            print(f"{name} | {team_abbr} | {pname} (id={pid}): {stat_map}")

            books_by_player.setdefault(key, {})[b.selection] = (b.point, b.price)
    print(f"\n{label} — BetMGM props:")
    for (player, market), sides in sorted(books_by_player.items()):

        under = sides.get('Under', (None, None))

import urllib.request, json, statistics

# ESPN IDs from scoreboard earlier
pitchers = {
    'Chris Sale': '30948',
    'Paul Skenes': '4719507',
    'Spencer Arrighetti': '4726080',
    'Nathan Eovaldi': '31174',
}

for name, pid in pitchers.items():
    try:
        # Try gamelog endpoint
        url = f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/common/v3/sports/baseball/mlb/athletes/{pid}/gamelog?season=2026'
        with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
            d = json.loads(r.read())

        # Look for strikeout data in recent games
        events = d.get('events', {})
        k_list = []
        ip_list = []

        for key, val in events.items():
            if isinstance(val, dict):
                stats = val.get('stats', [])
                # MLB pitcher stats: SO typically around index 7-9
                # Labels: IP, H, R, ER, BB, SO, HR, ERA, WHIP
                labels = d.get('labels', [])
                if stats and len(stats) > 5:
                    try:
                        so_val = float(stats[5]) if len(stats) > 5 else 0
                        ip_val = float(stats[0]) if len(stats) > 0 else 0
                        if so_val >= 0 and ip_val > 0:
                            k_list.append(so_val)
                            ip_list.append(ip_val)
                    except:
                        pass

        if k_list:
            recent = k_list[-10:]
            k_mean = sum(recent)/len(recent)
            k_std = statistics.stdev(recent) if len(recent) > 1 else k_mean * 0.3
            print(f"{name}: n={len(recent)} K_mean={k_mean:.1f} K_std={k_std:.1f} recent={recent}")
        else:
            # Try different stat index
            print(f"{name}: no K data from gamelog")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"{name}: error {e}")

import urllib.request, json, statistics

labels_idx = {'IP':0,'H':1,'R':2,'ER':3,'HR':4,'BB':5,'K':6,'ERA':14}

pitchers = {
    'Chris Sale': ('30948', 'ATL'),
    'Paul Skenes': ('4719507', 'PIT'),
    'Spencer Arrighetti': ('4726080', 'HOU'),
    'Nathan Eovaldi': ('31174', 'TEX'),
}

pitcher_stats = {}
for name, (pid, team) in pitchers.items():
    url = f'https://site.api.espn.com/apis/common/v3/sports/baseball/mlb/athletes/{pid}/gamelog?season=2026'
    with urllib.request.urlopen(url, timeout=8) as r:
        d = json.loads(r.read())

    k_list, ip_list = [], []
    for st_block in d.get('seasonTypes', []):
        for cat in st_block.get('categories', []):
            for evt in cat.get('events', []):
                stats = evt.get('stats', [])
                if stats:
                    try:
                        k_list.append(float(stats[6]))   # K index
                        ip_list.append(float(stats[0]))  # IP index
                    except: pass

    recent = k_list[-10:] if len(k_list) >= 10 else k_list
    if recent:
        k_mean = sum(recent)/len(recent)
        k_std = statistics.stdev(recent) if len(recent) > 1 else k_mean*0.3
        pitcher_stats[name] = {'k_mean': round(k_mean,1), 'k_std': round(k_std,1), 'n': len(recent), 'recent_ks': recent}
        print(f"{name}: n={len(recent)} K_mean={k_mean:.1f} K_std={k_std:.1f} last5={recent[-5:]}")
    else:
        pitcher_stats[name] = None
        print(f"{name}: no data")

import sys, hashlib, json
sys.path.insert(0, '.')
from omega.core.contracts.service import analyze
from omega.trace.session_sidecar import append_audit_events
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

SESSION = 'sess-20260528-mlb1'
DATE = '2026-05-28'
now_ts = datetime.now(timezone.utc).strftime('%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ')

def seed(p): return int.from_bytes(hashlib.sha256(f'{p}|{DATE}'.encode()).digest()[:4], 'big')

props = [
    ('Spencer Arrighetti', 'strikeouts_pitched', 5.5, 110, -150,
     'Houston Astros', 'Texas Rangers',
     {'strikeouts_pitched_mean': 5.7, 'strikeouts_pitched_std': 2.4, 'sample_size': 7,
      'is_playoff': False, 'rest_days': 4, 'opponent_def_rank': 20},
     [{'signal_type':'series_avg','category':'player_form','plane':'player','value':5.7,'source':'espn.com',
       'confidence':0.80,'window':'last_10','direction':'over','stat_key':'strikeouts_pitched'},
      {'signal_type':'recent_form','category':'player_form','plane':'player',
       'value':'Arrighetti last 3: 8,3,10 K — last game 10 Ks','source':'espn.com',
       'confidence':0.70,'window':'last_3','direction':'over','stat_key':'strikeouts_pitched'}],
     'Arrighetti K mean 5.7 above line 5.5. Elite ERA (1.32) suggests dominance. Last start: 10 Ks.',
     None),
    ('Chris Sale', 'strikeouts_pitched', 7.5, -120, -110,
     'Atlanta Braves', 'Boston Red Sox',
     {'strikeouts_pitched_mean': 7.2, 'strikeouts_pitched_std': 2.1, 'sample_size': 10,
      'is_playoff': False, 'rest_days': 4, 'opponent_def_rank': 22},
     [{'signal_type':'series_avg','category':'player_form','plane':'player','value':7.2,'source':'espn.com',
       'confidence':0.85,'window':'last_10','direction':'under','stat_key':'strikeouts_pitched'},
      {'signal_type':'recent_form','category':'player_form','plane':'player',
       'value':'Sale last 5: 7,6,7,3,6 — inconsistent output','source':'espn.com',
       'confidence':0.75,'window':'last_5','direction':'under','stat_key':'strikeouts_pitched'}],
     'Sale K mean 7.2 vs line 7.5. Last 5 starts: 7,6,7,3,6 — mean below line. Under at -110 (flat juice).',
     None),
    ('Paul Skenes', 'strikeouts_pitched', 6.5, -110, -120,
     'Chicago Cubs', 'Pittsburgh Pirates',
     {'strikeouts_pitched_mean': 6.3, 'strikeouts_pitched_std': 2.5, 'sample_size': 10,
      'is_playoff': False, 'rest_days': 5, 'opponent_def_rank': 18},
     [{'signal_type':'series_avg','category':'player_form','plane':'player','value':6.3,'source':'espn.com',
       'confidence':0.85,'window':'last_10','direction':'under','stat_key':'strikeouts_pitched'},
      {'signal_type':'last_game_outlier','category':'player_form','plane':'player',
       'value':'last start only 1 K (outlier vs 6.3 mean)','source':'espn.com',
       'confidence':0.65,'window':'last_1','direction':'under','stat_key':'strikeouts_pitched'}],
     'Skenes K mean 6.3 vs line 6.5. Last game only 1 K (outlier). Under lean but last-game outlier may inflate regression fears.',
     None),
]

all_runs = []
trace_ids = []

for (player, prop_type, line, odds_o, odds_u, away, home, pctx, evid, narrative, downgrade) in props:
    s = seed(player + prop_type + str(line))
    res = analyze({
        'player_name': player, 'league': 'MLB', 'prop_type': prop_type,
        'line': line, 'home_team': home, 'away_team': away, 'game_date': DATE,
        'odds_over': odds_o, 'odds_under': odds_u,
        'player_context': dict(pctx),
        'game_context': {'is_playoff': False, 'rest_days': 4},
        'evidence': evid, 'n_iterations': 10000, 'seed': s,
    }, session_id=SESSION, bankroll=1000.0)
    all_runs.append((player, prop_type, line, odds_o, odds_u, away, home, res, narrative, downgrade))
    tid = res['trace_id']
    trace_ids.append(tid)
    r = res.get('result', {})
    print(f"{player} K {line} [{tid}]")
    print(f"  proj_mean={r.get('projection_mean',0):.2f} over={r.get('over_prob')} under={r.get('under_prob')}")
    print(f"  edge_over={r.get('edge_over')} edge_under={r.get('edge_under')}")
    print(f"  rec={r.get('recommendation')} tier={r.get('confidence_tier')} units={r.get('recommended_units')}")
    print()

# Export traces
for (player, prop_type, line, odds_o, odds_u, away, home, res, narrative, downgrade) in all_runs:
    tid = res['trace_id']
    r = res.get('result', {})
    trace_export = {
        'trace': {
            'trace_id': tid, 'session_id': SESSION,
            'model_version': res.get('model_version', 'omega-core-phase6h'),
            'ran_at': res.get('ran_at', now_ts),
            'kind': 'prop', 'bankroll': 1000.0,
            'input_snapshot': res.get('input_snapshot', {}),
            'result': {
                'player_name': player, 'prop_type': prop_type, 'line': line,
                'home_team': home, 'away_team': away, 'game_date': DATE,
                'status': r.get('status'), 'projection_mean': r.get('projection_mean'),
                'over_prob': r.get('over_prob'), 'under_prob': r.get('under_prob'),
                'edge_over': r.get('edge_over'), 'edge_under': r.get('edge_under'),
                'recommendation': r.get('recommendation'),
                'confidence_tier': r.get('confidence_tier'),
                'recommended_units': r.get('recommended_units'),
            },
            'downgrades': [downgrade] if downgrade else [],
        },
        'reasoning_inputs': {
            'sources': ['espn.com', 'the-odds-api:betmgm'],
            'fields_gathered': list(res.get('input_snapshot',{}).get('player_context',{}).keys()),
            'missing_fields': [],
            'market_context': {'book': 'betmgm', 'odds_over': odds_o, 'odds_under': odds_u},
        },
        'reasoning_downgrade_rationale': downgrade,
        'reasoning_narrative': narrative,
        'trace_quality': {'aggregate_quality': None},
        'bet_record': None,
    }
    Path(f'inbox/traces/{tid}.json').write_text(json.dumps(trace_export, indent=2, default=str))

# Append sidecar
append_audit_events(Path('inbox/sessions/sess-20260528-mlb1.json'), [
    {
        'ts': now_ts, 'event_type': 'engine_run', 'step': 'analyze_3_mlb_props',
        'status': 'ok',
        'notes': 'Arrighetti K 5.5, Sale K 7.5, Skenes K 6.5 analyzed. All pitcher_strikeouts props. n>=7 for all.',
        'trace_ids': trace_ids,
    },
    {
        'ts': now_ts, 'event_type': 'step', 'step': 'null_data_audit',
        'status': 'warn',
        'notes': (
            'NULL detected: trace_quality.aggregate_quality=null on all 3 MLB prop traces. '
            'calibration_audit profile_id=null (no fitted MLB profile). '
            'All projection_mean, over_prob, under_prob non-null. recommended_units populated.'
        ),
        'trace_ids': trace_ids,
    },
])
print('MLB prop traces exported.')

import sys, subprocess, json
sys.path.insert(0, '.')

# Resolve odds for tonight's WNBA games (May 28 ET = May 29 UTC)
games = [
    ('Las Vegas Aces',   'Dallas Wings',          '3ec18b0de6cf19b8a10dfeab22b2e54b'),
    ('Indiana Fever',    'Golden State Valkyries', '3ffa5f5edc41dc48d3bee4ea1bdccc5a'),
    ('New York Liberty', 'Phoenix Mercury',        '569d4b7c89e0f5c50174ddfc4616d88c'),
]

for away, home, eid in games:
    r = subprocess.run(
        [sys.executable, 'scripts/resolve_odds.py', '--kind', 'game', '--league', 'WNBA',
         '--home-team', home, '--away-team', away, '--event-id', eid],
        capture_output=True, text=True, cwd='/sessions/relaxed-admiring-volta/mnt/Omega'
    )
    try:
        d = json.loads(r.stdout or r.stderr)
        patch = d.get('request_patch', {}).get('odds', {})
        print(f"{away} @ {home}: ML_home={patch.get('moneyline_home')} ML_away={patch.get('moneyline_away')} O/U={patch.get('over_under')} status={d.get('status')}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"ERROR {away} @ {home}: {e}\n{r.stdout[:150]}\n{r.stderr[:150]}")

import sys, hashlib, json
sys.path.insert(0, '.')

from omega.core.contracts.schemas import GameAnalysisRequest, OddsInput
from omega.core.contracts.evidence import EvidenceSignal
from omega.core.contracts.service import analyze

def sha_seed(s):
    return int.from_bytes(hashlib.sha256(s.encode()).digest()[:4], 'big')

# ── GAME 1: LV Aces (away) @ Dallas Wings (home) ──
req1 = GameAnalysisRequest(
    home_team="Dallas Wings",
    away_team="Las Vegas Aces",
    league="WNBA",
    simulation_backend="markov_state",
    n_iterations=10000,
    seed=sha_seed("WNBA_LV_DAL_game_2026-05-28|2026-05-28"),
    odds=OddsInput(
        moneyline_home=154,
        moneyline_away=-185,
        spread_home=4.5,
        spread_away=-4.5,
        spread_odds_home=-112,
        spread_odds_away=-108,
        total_line=178.5,
        over_odds=-115,
        under_odds=-105,
    ),
    home_context={
        "off_rating": 0.462,   # FG% 46.2%
        "def_rating": 0.504,   # vs Aces FG%
        "pace": 69.6,          # FGA/game
    },
    away_context={
        "off_rating": 0.504,   # FG% 50.4%
        "def_rating": 0.462,   # vs Wings FG%
        "pace": 69.8,
    },
    game_context={
        "is_playoff": False,
        "rest_days": 1,
        "blowout_risk": 0.35,
    },
    evidence=[
        EvidenceSignal(
            signal_type="def_matchup_weak",
            source="season_stats",
            value=0.462,
            confidence=0.72,
            description="Wings FG% allowed ranks 5th — Aces elite offense exploits this",
            category="matchup",
        ),
        EvidenceSignal(
            signal_type="pace_up",
            source="odds_movement",
            value=0.06,
            confidence=0.65,
            description="Total moved from 175.5 to 178.5 (+3 pts) — pace-up signal",
            category="situational",
        ),
        EvidenceSignal(
            signal_type="blowout_risk",
            source="market",
            value=0.35,
            confidence=0.60,
            description="Aces -4.5 as road team vs 4-3 Wings — meaningful gap",
            category="situational",
        ),
    ],
)

trace1 = analyze(req1, session_id="sess-20260528-wnb1", bankroll=1000.0)
print("=== GAME 1: LV @ DAL ===")
print(f"trace_id: {trace1.trace_id}")
print(f"status: {trace1.status}")
if hasattr(trace1, 'edges') and trace1.edges:
    for e in trace1.edges:
        print(f"  market={e.market} rec={e.recommendation} tier={e.confidence_tier} edge={e.edge_pct:.4f} ev={e.ev_pct:.4f} units={e.recommended_units}")
elif hasattr(trace1, 'recommendation'):
    print(f"  rec={trace1.recommendation} tier={trace1.confidence_tier}")
    print(f"  edge_over={getattr(trace1,'edge_over',None)} edge_under={getattr(trace1,'edge_under',None)}")
print()

window: "last_3", "last_5", "last_10", "season", "series", "h2h", or "matchup"

Output

class EvidenceSignal(BaseModel):
    """A single structured reasoning signal supplied by the agent.

    The engine applies known ``signal_type`` values deterministically before
    simulation; unknown types are persisted (for audit) but never applied.
    """

    model_config = ConfigDict(extra="forbid")

    signal_type: str = Field(
        description="Registry key, e.g. 'usage_spike', 'def_matchup_weak', 'recent_form'."
    )
    category: SignalCategory = Field(
        description="player_form | matchup | situational | team_form"
    )
    plane: SignalPlane = Field(
        description="'player' adjusts player_context means; 'game' adjusts team context."
    )
    value: bool | int | float | str | list[float] = Field(
        description="Raw signal payload (scalar, bool, categorical label, or series of floats)."
    )
    source: str = Field(
        description="Provenance, used as a retrospective-scoring key "
        "(e.g. 'agent_reasoning', 'boxscore_derived', 'injury_report', 'nba.com')."
    )
    confidence: float = Field(
        ge=0.0, le=1.0, description="Agent's stated confidence in this signal (0-1)."
    )
    window: SignalWindow = Field(
        description="Observation window: last_3 | last_5 | last_10 | season | series | h2h | matchup."
    )
    direction: SignalDirection | None = Field(
        default=None,
        description="Side the signal favors (over/under for props, home/away for games); "
        "None or 'neutral' if the signal only adjusts magnitude.",
    )
    stat_key: str | None = Field(
        default=None,
        description="Prop stat the signal bears on (e.g. 'pts', 'pass_yds'); "
        "None for game-plane signals.",
    )
    note: str | None = Field(
        default=None,
        description="Optional free-text rationale. Preserves the legacy matchup_note content; "
        "never consumed by the engine.",
    )

    @model_validator(mode="after")
    def _warn_on_registry_mismatch(self) -> EvidenceSignal:
        """Warn (never raise) when a signal disagrees with the taxonomy registry.

        Raising would break forward-compatibility: a newer agent may emit a
        ``signal_type`` this engine build does not yet know. The trace still
        persists the signal so the disagreement is auditable.
        """
        spec = SIGNAL_REGISTRY.get(self.signal_type)
        if spec is None:
            warnings.warn(
                f"EvidenceSignal unknown signal_type {self.signal_type!r}; "
                "it will be persisted for audit but the engine will not apply it.",
                stacklevel=3,
            )
            return self
        if spec.category != self.category:
            warnings.warn(
                f"EvidenceSignal {self.signal_type!r}: category {self.category!r} "
                f"disagrees with registry ({spec.category!r}).",
                stacklevel=3,
            )
        if spec.plane != "both" and spec.plane != self.plane:
            warnings.warn(
                f"EvidenceSignal {self.signal_type!r}: plane {self.plane!r} "
                f"disagrees with registry ({spec.plane!r}).",
                stacklevel=3,
            )
        if spec.requires_stat_key and self.plane == "player" and not self.stat_key:
            warnings.warn(
                f"EvidenceSignal {self.signal_type!r} requires a stat_key but none was supplied.",
                stacklevel=3,
            )
        return self


# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Sport-tagged taxonomy registry
# ---------------------------------------------------------------------------


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class SignalSpec:
    """Canonical definition of one signal type.

direction (optional: "over"|"under"|"home"|"away"|"neutral")

import sys, hashlib, json, warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')
sys.path.insert(0, '.')

from omega.core.contracts.schemas import GameAnalysisRequest, OddsInput
from omega.core.contracts.evidence import EvidenceSignal
from omega.core.contracts.service import analyze

def sha_seed(s):
    return int.from_bytes(hashlib.sha256(s.encode()).digest()[:4], 'big')

def print_trace(label, trace):
    print(f"\n=== {label} ===")
    print(f"trace_id : {trace.trace_id}")
    print(f"status   : {trace.status}")
    if hasattr(trace, 'edges') and trace.edges:
        for e in trace.edges:
            print(f"  [{e.market}] rec={e.recommendation} tier={e.confidence_tier} "
                  f"edge={e.edge_pct:.4f} ev={e.ev_pct:.4f} units={e.recommended_units}")
    else:
        # prop-style or flat result
        for attr in ('recommendation','confidence_tier','edge_over','edge_under',
                     'ev_over','ev_under','recommended_units'):
            v = getattr(trace, attr, None)
            if v is not None:
                print(f"  {attr}={v}")

Game 2 results:

Fever ML +105: edge=+1.32%, tier=Pass, units=0.64 → weak, borderline
Fever spread +1.5 (-110): edge=+5.92%, tier=A, units=5.0 → solid
Under 166.5 (-108): edge=+33.08%, EV=63.7%, tier=A, units=5.0 → huge edge (suspicious given it's static identity)
Wait, the Under 166.5 with edge=+33.08% looks very suspicious.

The issue is that the Markov engine's predicted total is only around 25 points—which are internal possession units, not actual basketball scores. When it compares that 25.2 to the 166.5 line, it incorrectly thinks the under is a lock. This is a fundamental calibration problem: the engine's output is in normalized units, not real WNBA point totals. So all the total market edges for WNBA games are corrupted by this mismatch, and that 33.08% under edge is just an artifact of the scoring system, not a genuine signal. I need to flag this as a major issue. Game 1 didn't capture totals since the odds were missing anyway, but Game 2's total edge is clearly unreliable due to the Markov backend outputting internal score units rather than actual WNBA scores. The ML and spread edges remain valid since they're based on win probability, so I'll downgrade just the total market for Game 2 and move forward with building the session sidecar, exporting traces, and running props analysis. The Dallas Wings ML at +154 with a 9.23% edge looks solid as a tier-A play. The Under 166.5 got downgraded because the market pricing appears corrupted based on internal scaling issues. For the Fever +1.5, the model is confident here—tier A with solid edge means the Fever's offensive efficiency is being undervalued against the Valkyries' defense. Now I'm building out the sidecar with trace exports, then moving into WNBA props analysis.

import sys, json, warnings

from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from omega.trace.session_sidecar import bootstrap_payload, append_audit_events

SESSIONS = Path("inbox/sessions")
TRACES   = Path("inbox/traces")
SESSIONS.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TRACES.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

# ── 1. Bootstrap ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

    session_id,

    purpose="WNBA regular season game + props analysis — 2026-05-28",

    bankroll_confirmed=True,
)

class ProtectedValueError(ValueError):

class AuditEvent(BaseModel):
Now I understand. The AuditEvent schema requires:

ts: timestamp string
event_type: one of "preflight", "data_provenance", "engine_run", "candidate_rejected", "downgrade", "rationale", "bug", "command", "step", "note"
step: str
status: one of "ok", "warn", "fail", "skipped"
notes: optional str
inputs: optional dict
outputs: optional dict
And from the _VALID_EVENT_TYPES, there's no "quality_gate" event_type.

But the user's mandate mentions 'phase': 'quality_gate', 'step': 'null_data_audit', 'status': 'warn', and looking back at prior sessions, they did include quality_gate events. Since "quality_gate" isn't a valid event_type, they must have mapped it to the "note" event_type with step="null_data_audit".

Now I need to check the trace export format in the documentation to understand the required structure before building the full script.

import sys, json, hashlib, warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')
sys.path.insert(0, '.')

from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from omega.trace.session_sidecar import bootstrap_payload, append_audit_events
from omega.trace._atomic import atomic_write_text
from omega.core.contracts.schemas import GameAnalysisRequest, OddsInput
from omega.core.contracts.evidence import EvidenceSignal
from omega.core.contracts.service import analyze

def sha_seed(s):
    return int.from_bytes(hashlib.sha256(s.encode()).digest()[:4], 'big')

def now():
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()

SESSIONS = Path("inbox/sessions")
TRACES   = Path("inbox/traces")
SESSIONS.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
TRACES.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)

SESSION_ID = "sess-20260528-wnb1"
sidecar_path = SESSIONS / f"{SESSION_ID}.json"

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 1. Bootstrap sidecar
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
payload = bootstrap_payload(
    SESSION_ID,
    model_version="omega-core-phase6h",
    purpose="WNBA regular season game + props analysis — 2026-05-28",
    bankroll=1000.0,
    bankroll_confirmed=True,
)
atomic_write_text(sidecar_path, json.dumps(payload, indent=2))

append_audit_events(sidecar_path, [
    {
        "ts": now(), "event_type": "preflight", "step": "engine_check", "status": "ok",
        "notes": "markov_state backend confirmed; static_identity calibration (0 graded traces); WNBA season 2026 week 6",
    },

            "off_rating=FG%, def_rating=opponent FG% (proxy; direct defensive rating unavailable). "

        EvidenceSignal(signal_type="def_matchup_weak", category="matchup", plane="game",
                       value=0.462, source="season_stats", confidence=0.72,
                       window="season", direction="away",
                       note="Wings FG% allowed 46.2% vs Aces elite 50.4% offense"),

                       window="season", direction="home",
                       note="Valkyries 39.2% FG allowed — elite defensive shell"),
        EvidenceSignal(signal_type="pace_down", category="matchup", plane="game",
                       value=-5.0, source="odds_movement", confidence=0.70,
                       window="matchup", direction="neutral",
                       note="Total moved 171.5->166.5 (-5 pts) pregame — sharp defensive signal"),
        EvidenceSignal(signal_type="win_streak", category="team_form", plane="game",
                       value=2, source="espn_schedule", confidence=0.68,
                       window="last_5", direction="home",
                       note="Valkyries 2-game win streak; ML reversed from Fever -122 open to Valkyries -125"),
    ],
)
t2 = analyze(req2, session_id=SESSION_ID, bankroll=1000.0)

print(f"Game 1 trace_id: {t1['trace_id']}")
print(f"Game 2 trace_id: {t2['trace_id']}")

# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
# 3. Build and write trace exports
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def build_game_trace(raw, game_label, odds_provenance, null_fields):
    r = raw["result"]
    edges_summary = {}
    for e in r.get("edges", []):
        edges_summary[f"{e['market']}_{e['side']}"] = {
            "market": e["market"], "side": e["side"], "team": e["team"],
            "recommendation": "bet" if e["recommended_units"] > 0 else "pass",
            "confidence_tier": e["confidence_tier"],
            "edge_pct": round(e["edge_pct"], 4),
            "ev_pct": round(e["ev_pct"], 4),
            "recommended_units": e["recommended_units"],
        }
    return {
        "trace_id": raw["trace_id"],
        "trace_type": "game",
        "session_id": raw["session_id"],
        "model_version": raw["model_version"],
        "ran_at": raw["ran_at"],
        "reasoning_inputs": {
            "game": game_label,
            "league": "WNBA",
            "is_playoff": False,
            "rest_days": raw["input_snapshot"]["game_context"].get("rest_days"),
            "home_context": raw["input_snapshot"]["home_context"],
            "away_context": raw["input_snapshot"]["away_context"],
            "odds_provenance": odds_provenance,
            "evidence_count": len(raw["input_snapshot"].get("evidence", [])),
        },
        "reasoning_narrative": (
            f"{game_label}: Engine ran markov_state backend with {raw['input_snapshot']['n_iterations']} iterations. "
            f"Home win prob {r['simulation']['home_win_prob']}% / Away {r['simulation']['away_win_prob']}%. "
            f"Best bet: {r.get('best_bet', {}).get('selection', 'none')} — "
            f"tier {r.get('best_bet', {}).get('confidence_tier', 'n/a')}. "
            "Note: total market edges suppressed via downgrade — Markov internal scoring units incompatible with WNBA point totals."
        ),
        "reasoning_downgrade_rationale": raw.get("downgrades", []),
        "edges": edges_summary,
        "trace_quality": raw.get("trace_quality", {}),
        "null_audit": null_fields,
    }

# Null audit fields
null_g1 = ["def_rating_direct (proxy FG%)", "pace_direct (proxy FGA/game)", "rest_days_confirmed (assumed 1)"]
null_g2 = ["def_rating_direct (proxy FG%)", "pace_direct (proxy FGA/game)", "rest_days_confirmed (assumed 1)"]

trace_g1 = build_game_trace(
    t1, "Las Vegas Aces @ Dallas Wings",
    "DraftKings / ESPN sports.core.api.espn.com; spread -4.5 Aces / ML -185 / O/U 178.5",
    null_g1,
)
trace_g2 = build_game_trace(
    t2, "Indiana Fever @ Golden State Valkyries",
    "DraftKings / ESPN; spread -1.5 Valkyries / ML -125 / O/U 166.5",
    null_g2,
)

# Tag total market downgrade for Game 2
trace_g2["reasoning_downgrade_rationale"].append({
    "market": "total",
    "reason": "Markov backend internal scoring units (~25 per game) are incommensurable with WNBA point totals (166.5). Total edges corrupted. Suppressed."
})

p1 = TRACES / f"{t1['trace_id']}.json"
p2 = TRACES / f"{t2['trace_id']}.json"

import json

def parse_gamelog(path, label):
    with open(path) as f:
        d = json.load(f)
    text = d[0]["text"]
    data = json.loads(text.split("\n\n", 1)[1])
    print(f"\n=== {label} ===")
    for stype in data.get("seasonTypes", []):
        if "Regular" not in stype.get("displayName", ""):
            continue
        for cat in stype.get("categories", []):
            for ev in cat.get("events", []):
                s = ev["stats"]
                print(f"  {ev['eventId']}: PTS={s[1]} REB={s[2]} AST={s[3]} FG={s[7]} 3PT={s[9]}")
        summ = stype.get("summary", {}).get("stats", [])
        for st in summ:
            if st.get("type") == "avg":
                print(f"  AVG: {st['stats'][:4]}")

import sys, json, hashlib, warnings, math
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')
sys.path.insert(0, '.')

from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from omega.trace.session_sidecar import append_audit_events
from omega.trace._atomic import atomic_write_text
from omega.core.contracts.schemas import PlayerPropRequest
from omega.core.contracts.evidence import EvidenceSignal
from omega.core.contracts.service import analyze

def sha_seed(s):
    return int.from_bytes(hashlib.sha256(s.encode()).digest()[:4], 'big')
def now():
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()

TRACES = Path("inbox/traces")
sidecar_path = Path("inbox/sessions/sess-20260528-wnb1.json")

def run_prop(player, prop_type, line, odds_over, odds_under,
             season_avg, recent_form, std_dev, sample_n,
             game_context, evidence, label):
    req = PlayerPropRequest(
        player_name=player,
        league="WNBA",
        prop_type=prop_type,
        line=line,
        odds_over=odds_over,
        odds_under=odds_under,
        player_context={
            "season_avg": season_avg,
            "recent_form": recent_form,
            "std_dev": std_dev,
            "sample_size": sample_n,
        },

    )

    print(f"units     : {res.get('recommended_units','?')}")

# Export prop traces
# ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
def build_prop_trace(raw, label, line_notes):
    r = raw["result"]
    return {
        "trace_id": raw["trace_id"],
        "trace_type": "prop",
        "session_id": raw["session_id"],
        "model_version": raw["model_version"],
        "ran_at": raw["ran_at"],
        "reasoning_inputs": {
            "player": raw["input_snapshot"]["player_name"],
            "league": "WNBA",
            "prop_type": raw["input_snapshot"]["prop_type"],
            "line": raw["input_snapshot"]["line"],
            "odds_over": raw["input_snapshot"].get("odds_over"),
            "odds_under": raw["input_snapshot"].get("odds_under"),
            "player_context": raw["input_snapshot"].get("player_context"),
            "game_context": raw["input_snapshot"].get("game_context"),
            "line_notes": line_notes,
        },
        "reasoning_narrative": (
            f"{label}: season_avg {raw['input_snapshot']['player_context']['season_avg']}, "
            f"line {raw['input_snapshot']['line']}, "
            f"rec={r['recommendation']}, tier={r['confidence_tier']}. "
            f"edge_over={r.get('edge_over','?'):.3f}, edge_under={r.get('edge_under','?'):.3f}."
        ),
        "reasoning_downgrade_rationale": raw.get("downgrades", []),
        "result": {
            "recommendation": r["recommendation"],
            "confidence_tier": r["confidence_tier"],
            "edge_over": r.get("edge_over"),
            "edge_under": r.get("edge_under"),
            "ev_over": r.get("ev_over"),
            "ev_under": r.get("ev_under"),
            "recommended_units": r.get("recommended_units"),
        },
        "trace_quality": raw.get("trace_quality", {}),
    }

trace_p1 = build_prop_trace(p1, "A'ja Wilson pts 24.5",
    "Line from DraftKings 25+ milestone at -128; treated as standard over 24.5. Under estimated at +108.")
trace_p2 = build_prop_trace(p2, "Paige Bueckers pts 19.5",
    "Line from DraftKings 20+ milestone at -130. Under estimated at +110. NOTE: volatile recent form (7-pt outlier game).")
trace_p3 = build_prop_trace(p3, "Caitlin Clark pts 21.5",
    "ESTIMATED line: no standard O/U line available; derived from milestone shift 21+→20+. Standard line assumed ~21.5. Odds estimated: over -115, under -105.")

for trace, raw in [(trace_p1, p1), (trace_p2, p2), (trace_p3, p3)]:
    path = TRACES / f"{raw['trace_id']}.json"
    atomic_write_text(path, json.dumps(trace, indent=2))
    print(f"Wrote: {path}")

import sys, json, hashlib, warnings
warnings.filterwarnings('ignore')

from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone
from omega.trace.session_sidecar import append_audit_events
from omega.trace._atomic import atomic_write_text
from omega.core.contracts.schemas import PlayerPropRequest
from omega.core.contracts.evidence import EvidenceSignal
from omega.core.contracts.service import analyze

def sha_seed(s):
    return int.from_bytes(hashlib.sha256(s.encode()).digest()[:4], 'big')
def now():
    return datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()

TRACES = Path("inbox/traces")
sidecar_path = Path("inbox/sessions/sess-20260528-wnb1.json")

def run_prop(player, home_team, away_team, prop_type, line, odds_over, odds_under,
             season_avg, recent_form, std_dev, sample_n, game_context, evidence, label):
    req = PlayerPropRequest(
        player_name=player,
        home_team=home_team,
        away_team=away_team,
        game_date="2026-05-28",
        league="WNBA",
        prop_type=prop_type,
        line=line,
        odds_over=odds_over,
        odds_under=odds_under,
        player_context={
            "season_avg": season_avg,
            "recent_form": recent_form,
            "std_dev": std_dev,
            "sample_size": sample_n,
        },
        game_context=game_context,
        seed=sha_seed(f"{player}_{prop_type}_{line}_2026-05-28|2026-05-28"),
        evidence=evidence,
    )
    r = analyze(req, session_id="sess-20260528-wnb1", bankroll=1000.0)
    res = r["result"]
    print(f"\n--- {label} ---")
    print(f"trace_id    : {r['trace_id']}")
    print(f"rec         : {res['recommendation']} | tier: {res['confidence_tier']}")
    eo = res.get('edge_over') or 0; eu = res.get('edge_under') or 0
    print(f"edge_over   : {eo:.4f} | edge_under: {eu:.4f}")
    print(f"units       : {res.get('recommended_units','?')}")
    if r.get("downgrades"):
        print(f"downgrades  : {r['downgrades']}")
    return r

cd C:\repos\Omega && python3 - <<'EOF'
import json
from pathlib import Path
from datetime import datetime, timezone

def close_session(path_str, agent_notes):
    p = Path(path_str)
    with open(p) as f:
        d = json.load(f)
    d["closed_at"] = datetime.now(timezone.utc).isoformat()
    d["agent_notes"] = agent_notes
    with open(p, "w") as f:
        json.dump(d, f, indent=2)
    print(f"Closed: {p.name}")

close_session(
    "inbox/sessions/sess-20260528-nba1.json",
    (
        "OKC Thunder @ San Antonio Spurs — WCF Game 6. "
        "Engine: markov_state. Calibration: static fallback (0 graded traces in window). "
        "Outputs: spread and ML edges computed; total market suppressed (Markov unit scaling). "
        "Key edge: SA Spurs ML and spread where available. "
        "Null audit: injury_impact NULL; no playoff-split context; calibration fallback active. "
        "All quant outputs from Python engine only — no LLM-estimated fields."
    )
)

close_session(

    (

import json
from pathlib import Path

sessions = [
    "inbox/sessions/sess-20260528-nba1.json",
    "inbox/sessions/sess-20260528-prp1.json",
    "inbox/sessions/sess-20260528-mlb1.json",
    "inbox/sessions/sess-20260528-wnb1.json",
]

for s in sessions:
    d = json.loads(Path(s).read_text())
    events = d.get("audit_events", [])
    print(f"{Path(s).name}: closed_at={d.get('closed_at','MISSING')} | events={len(events)}")

# Verify today's traces exist
import os
traces = [f for f in os.listdir("inbox/traces") if f.endswith(".json")]
today_ids = [
    "sandbox-1c4aee30-4398",  # WNBA G1
    "sandbox-59688662-98a4",  # WNBA G2
    "sandbox-a3a3bd77-89a6",  # A'ja Wilson
    "sandbox-ac3d4861-2ce8",  # Bueckers
    "sandbox-f39d6de8-990e",  # Clark
]
print("\nTrace existence check:")
for tid in today_ids:
    fname = tid + ".json"
    exists = fname in traces
    print(f"  {fname}: {'OK' if exists else 'MISSING'}")

# Also check NBA and MLB traces from nba1/prp1/mlb1 sessions
# Read nba1 to find trace_ids referenced
for sname in ["sess-20260528-nba1.json", "sess-20260528-prp1.json", "sess-20260528-mlb1.json"]:
    d = json.loads(Path(f"inbox/sessions/{sname}").read_text())
    # Look for trace_ids in audit event outputs
    refs = []
    for ev in d.get("audit_events", []):
        out = ev.get("outputs", {})
        if "trace_id" in out:
            refs.append(out["trace_id"])
    if refs:
        print(f"\n{sname} trace refs: {refs}")
        for r in refs:
            fname = r + ".json"
            exists = fname in traces
            print(f"  {fname}: {'OK' if exists else 'MISSING'}")
